<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***homo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:home.html>homo</a> (11230)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1"><a href = vnd.unilang:etymology.html>Etymology</a> 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:clipping.html>clipping</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:word.html>words</a> prefixed <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">homo-</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὁμο-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">homo-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:same.html>same</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>i</a>.<a href = vnd.unilang:e.html>e</a>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">homogenized</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:homosexual.html>homosexual</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
